Success/Advantage\n    'yellow': RGBColor(255, 193, 7),   # Warning/Adequate\n    'red': RGBColor(244, 67, 54),      # Error/Concern\n    'blue': RGBColor(33, 150, 243),    # Info/Neutral\n    'dark_gray': RGBColor(66, 66, 66), # Text\n}\n\nTEMPLATE_PATH = r\"S:\\OneDrive - Safari Circuits, LLC\\Information Technology - Documents\\Grand Rapids IT Hub\\10_Templates\\01_PPT_Template.pptx\"\n\n\ndef load_config(config_file: Path) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n    \"\"\"Load presentation configuration from YAML or JSON file.\"\"\"\n    with open(config_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n        if config_file.suffix in ['.yaml', '.yml']:\n            return yaml.safe_load(f)\n        elif config_file.suffix == '.json':\n            return json.load(f)\n        else:\n            raise ValueError(f\"Unsupported config format: {config_file.suffix}\")\n\n\ndef add_title_slide(prs: Presentation, config: Dict) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Add title slide.\"\"\"\n    slide = prs.slides.add_slide(prs.slide_layouts[0])  # Title slide layout\n\n    title = slide.shapes.title\n    subtitle = slide.placeholders[1]\n\n    title.text = config.get('title', '')\n    subtitle.text = config.get('subtitle', '')\n\n\ndef add_section_header(prs: Presentation, title: str) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Add section header slide.\"\"\"\n    slide = prs.slides.add_slide(prs.slide_layouts[2])  # Section header layout\n    slide.shapes.title.text = title\n\n\ndef add_content_slide(prs: Presentation, slide_config: Dict) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Add content slide with title and bullet points.\"\"\"\n    slide = prs.slides.add_slide(prs.slide_layouts[1])  # Title and content layout\n\n    title = slide.shapes.title\n    title.text = slide_config.get('title', '')\n\n    # Add content to text placeholder\n    if 'content' in slide_config:\n        body_shape = slide.placeholders[1]\n        tf = body_shape.text_frame\n        tf.clear()\n\n        for item in slide_config['content']:\n            p = tf.add_paragraph()\n            p.text = item\n            p.level = 0\n\n\ndef add_comparison_table(prs: Presentation, slide_config: Dict) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Add comparison table slide.\"\"\"\n    slide = prs.slides.add_slide(prs.slide_layouts[5])  # Blank layout\n\n    # Add title\n    title_shape = slide.shapes.title\n    title_shape.text = slide_config.get('title', '')\n\n    # Table dimensions\n    rows = len(slide_config['rows']) + 1  # +1 for header\n    cols = len(slide_config['columns'])\n\n    # Create table\n    left = Inches(0.5)\n    top = Inches(1.5)\n    width = Inches(9.0)\n    height = Inches(0.5 * rows)\n\n    table = slide.shapes.add_table(rows, cols, left, top, width, height).table\n\n    # Set column headers\n    for col_idx, col_name in enumerate(slide_config['columns']):\n        cell = table.cell(0, col_idx)\n        cell.text = col_name\n        cell.text_frame.paragraphs[0].font.bold = True\n        cell.text_frame.paragraphs[0].alignment = PP_ALIGN.CENTER\n\n    # Fill table data\n    for row_idx, row_data in enumerate(slide_config['rows'], start=1):\n        for col_idx, cell_value in enumerate(row_data):\n            cell = table.cell(row_idx, col_idx)\n\n            # Handle colored cells (e.g., \"🟢 YES\", \"🔴 NO\")\n            if isinstance(cell_value, str):\n                cell.text = cell_value\n\n                # Apply color coding\n                if '🟢' in cell_value or 'YES' in cell_value.upper():\n                    cell.fill.solid()\n                    cell.fill.fore_color.rgb = COLORS['green']\n                elif '🔴' in cell_value or 'NO' in cell_value.upper():\n                    cell.fill.solid()\n                    cell.fill.fore_color.rgb = COLORS['red']\n                elif '🟡' in cell_value:\n                    cell.fill.solid()\n                    cell.fill.fore_color.rgb = COLORS['yellow']\n\n\ndef add_cost_chart_slide(prs: Presentation, slide_config: Dict) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Add cost comparison chart slide.\"\"\"\n    slide = prs.slides.add_slide(prs.slide_layouts[5])  # Blank layout\n\n    title_shape = slide.shapes.title\n    title_shape.text = slide_config.get('title', '')\n\n    # For now, add as table - could be enhanced with actual charts\n    # This would require more complex chart creation with python-pptx\n    add_comparison_table(prs, slide_config)\n\n\ndef generate_presentation(config_file: Path, output_file: Path) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Generate PowerPoint presentation from configuration file.\"\"\"\n\n    print(f\"Loading configuration from: {config_file}\")\n    config = load_config(config_file)\n\n    print(f\"Loading template from: {TEMPLATE_PATH}\")\n    prs = Presentation(TEMPLATE_PATH)\n\n    # Add title slide\n    if 'title_slide' in config:\n        add_title_slide(prs, config['title_slide'])\n\n    # Process slides\n    for slide_config in config.get('slides', []):\n        slide_type = slide_config.get('type', 'content')\n\n        if slide_type == 'section_header':\n            add_section_header(prs, slide_config['title'])\n        elif slide_type == 'content':\n            add_content_slide(prs, slide_config)\n        elif slide_type == 'table':\n            add_comparison_table(prs, slide_config)\n        elif slide_type == 'cost_chart':\n            add_cost_chart_slide(prs, slide_config)\n        else:\n            print(f\"Warning: Unknown slide type '{slide_type}', skipping\")\n\n    # Save presentation\n    print(f\"Saving presentation to: {output_file}\")\n    prs.save(str(output_file))\n    print(\"✓ Presentation generated successfully!\")\n\n\ndef main():\n    import argparse\n\n    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(\n        description='Generate Safari Circuits PowerPoint presentations from YAML/JSON config'\n    )\n    parser.add_argument('config', type=Path, help='Configuration file (YAML or JSON)')\n    parser.add_argument('-o', '--output', type=Path, help='Output PPTX file')\n\n    args = parser.parse_args()\n\n    if not args.config.exists():\n        print(f\"Error: Configuration file not found: {args.config}\")\n        return 1\n\n    if not args.output:\n        args.output = args.config.with_suffix('.pptx')\n\n    try:\n        generate_presentation(args.config, args.output)\n        return 0\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"Error generating presentation: {e}\")\n        import traceback\n        traceback.print_exc()\n        return 1\n\n\nif __name__ == '__main__':\n    exit(main())\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"stop_details":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":8,"cache_creation_input_tokens":387,"cache_read_input_tokens":53916,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":387},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"}},"requestId":"req_011Cax4P1um68jKzbpznMKwQ","type":"assistant","uuid":"1cebd401-78c3-449d-94e4-fe20c3e71729","timestamp":"2026-05-12T04:40:37.585Z"}

Success/Advantage\n    'yellow': RGBColor(255, 193, 7),   # Warning/Adequate\n    'red': RGBColor(244, 67, 54),      # Error/Concern\n    'blue': RGBColor(33, 150, 243),    # Info/Neutral\n    'dark_gray': RGBColor(66, 66, 66), # Title and content layout\n\n    title = slide.shapes.title\n    title.text = slide_config.get('title', '')\n\n    # Add content to text placeholder\n    if 'content' in slide_config:\n        body_shape = slide.placeholders[1]\n        tf = body_shape.text_frame\n        tf.clear()\n\n        for item in slide_config['content']:\n            p = tf.add_paragraph()\n            p.text = item\n            p.level = 0\n\n\ndef add_comparison_table(prs: Presentation, slide_config: Dict) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Add comparison table slide.\"\"\"\n    slide = prs.slides.add_slide(prs.slide_layouts[5])  # Blank layout\n\n    # Add title\n    title_shape = slide.shapes.title\n    title_shape.text = slide_config.get('title', '')\n\n    # Table dimensions\n    rows = len(slide_config['rows']) + 1  # +1 for header\n    cols = len(slide_config['columns'])\n\n    # Create table\n    left = Inches(0.5)\n    top = Inches(1.5)\n    width = Inches(9.0)\n    height = Inches(0.5 * rows)\n\n    table = slide.shapes.add_table(rows, cols, left, top, width, height).table\n\n    # Set column headers\n    for col_idx, col_name in enumerate(slide_config['columns']):\n        cell = table.cell(0, col_idx)\n        cell.text = col_name\n        cell.text_frame.paragraphs[0].font.bold = True\n        cell.text_frame.paragraphs[0].alignment = PP_ALIGN.CENTER\n\n    # Fill table data\n    for row_idx, row_data in enumerate(slide_config['rows'], start=1):\n        for col_idx, cell_value in enumerate(row_data):\n            cell = table.cell(row_idx, col_idx)\n\n            # Handle colored cells (e.g., \"🟢 YES\", \"🔴 NO\")\n            if isinstance(cell_value, str):\n                cell.text = cell_value\n\n                # Apply color coding\n                if '🟢' in cell_value or 'YES' in cell_value.upper():\n                    cell.fill.solid()\n                    cell.fill.fore_color.rgb = COLORS['green']\n                elif '🔴' in cell_value or 'NO' in cell_value.upper():\n                    cell.fill.solid()\n                    cell.fill.fore_color.rgb = COLORS['red']\n                elif '🟡' in cell_value:\n                    cell.fill.solid()\n                    cell.fill.fore_color.rgb = COLORS['yellow']\n\n\ndef add_cost_chart_slide(prs: Presentation, slide_config: Dict) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Add cost comparison chart slide.\"\"\"\n    slide = prs.slides.add_slide(prs.slide_layouts[5])  # Add title slide\n    if 'title_slide' in config:\n        add_title_slide(prs, config['title_slide'])\n\n    # Process slides\n    for slide_config in config.get('slides', []):\n        slide_type = slide_config.get('type', 'content')\n\n        if slide_type == 'section_header':\n            add_section_header(prs, slide_config['title'])\n        elif slide_type == 'content':\n            add_content_slide(prs, slide_config)\n        elif slide_type == 'table':\n            add_comparison_table(prs, slide_config)\n        elif slide_type == 'cost_chart':\n            add_cost_chart_slide(prs, slide_config)\n        else:\n            print(f\"Warning: Unknown slide type '{slide_type}', skipping\")\n\n    # Section header layout\n    slide.shapes.title.text = title\n\n\ndef add_content_slide(prs: Presentation, slide_config: Dict) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Add content slide with title and bullet points.\"\"\"\n    slide = prs.slides.add_slide(prs.slide_layouts[1])  # Title and content layout\n\n    title = slide.shapes.title\n    title.text = slide_config.get('title', '')\n\n    # Add content to text placeholder\n    if 'content' in slide_config:\n        body_shape = slide.placeholders[1]\n        tf = body_shape.text_frame\n        tf.clear()\n\n        for item in slide_config['content']:\n            p = tf.add_paragraph()\n            p.text = item\n            p.level = 0\n\n\ndef add_comparison_table(prs: Presentation, slide_config: Dict) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Add comparison table slide.\"\"\"\n    slide = prs.slides.add_slide(prs.slide_layouts[5])  # Blank layout\n\n    # Add title\n    title_shape = slide.shapes.title\n    title_shape.text = slide_config.get('title', '')\n\n    # Table dimensions\n    rows = len(slide_config['rows']) + 1  # +1 for header\n    cols = len(slide_config['columns'])\n\n    # Create table\n    left = Inches(0.5)\n    top = Inches(1.5)\n    width = Inches(9.0)\n    height = Inches(0.5 * rows)\n\n    table = slide.shapes.add_table(rows, cols, left, top, width, height).table\n\n    # Set column headers\n    for col_idx, col_name in enumerate(slide_config['columns']):\n        cell = table.cell(0, col_idx)\n        cell.text = col_name\n        cell.text_frame.paragraphs[0].font.bold = True\n        cell.text_frame.paragraphs[0].alignment = PP_ALIGN.CENTER\n\n    # Fill table data\n    for row_idx, row_data in enumerate(slide_config['rows'], start=1):\n        for col_idx, cell_value in enumerate(row_data):\n            cell = table.cell(row_idx, col_idx)\n\n            # Handle colored cells (e.g., \"🟢 YES\", \"🔴 NO\")\n            if isinstance(cell_value, str):\n                cell.text = cell_value\n\n                # Apply color coding\n                if '🟢' in cell_value or 'YES' in cell_value.upper():\n                    cell.fill.solid()\n                    cell.fill.fore_color.rgb = COLORS['green']\n                elif '🔴' in cell_value or 'NO' in cell_value.upper():\n                    cell.fill.solid()\n                    cell.fill.fore_color.rgb = COLORS['red']\n                elif '🟡' in cell_value:\n                    cell.fill.solid()\n                    cell.fill.fore_color.rgb = COLORS['yellow']\n\n\ndef add_cost_chart_slide(prs: Presentation, slide_config: Dict) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Add cost comparison chart slide.\"\"\"\n    slide = prs.slides.add_slide(prs.slide_layouts[5])  # Blank layout\n\n    title_shape = slide.shapes.title\n    title_shape.text = slide_config.get('title', '')\n\n    # For now, add as table - could be enhanced with actual charts\n    # This would require more complex chart creation with python-pptx\n    add_comparison_table(prs, slide_config)\n\n\ndef generate_presentation(config_file: Path, output_file: Path) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Generate PowerPoint presentation from configuration file.\"\"\"\n\n    print(f\"Loading configuration from: {config_file}\")\n    config = load_config(config_file)\n\n    print(f\"Loading template from: {TEMPLATE_PATH}\")\n    prs = Presentation(TEMPLATE_PATH)\n\n    # Add title slide\n    if 'title_slide' in config:\n        add_title_slide(prs, config['title_slide'])\n\n    # Process slides\n    for slide_config in config.get('slides', []):\n        slide_type = slide_config.get('type', 'content')\n\n        if slide_type == 'section_header':\n            add_section_header(prs, slide_config['title'])\n        elif slide_type == 'content':\n            add_content_slide(prs, slide_config)\n        elif slide_type == 'table':\n            add_comparison_table(prs, slide_config)\n        elif slide_type == 'cost_chart':\n            add_cost_chart_slide(prs, slide_config)\n        else:\n            print(f\"Warning: Unknown slide type '{slide_type}', skipping\")\n\n    # Save presentation\n    print(f\"Saving presentation to: {output_file}\")\n    prs.save(str(output_file))\n    print(\"✓ Presentation generated successfully!\")\n\n\ndef main():\n    import argparse\n\n    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(\n        description='Generate Safari Circuits PowerPoint presentations from YAML/JSON config'\n    )\n    parser.add_argument('config', type=Path, help='Configuration file (YAML or JSON)')\n    parser.add_argument('-o', '--output', type=Path, help='Output PPTX file')\n\n    args = parser.parse_args()\n\n    if not args.config.exists():\n        print(f\"Error: Configuration file not found: {args.config}\")\n        return 1\n\n    if not args.output:\n        args.output = args.config.with_suffix('.pptx')\n\n    try:\n        generate_presentation(args.config, args.output)\n        return 0\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"Error generating presentation: {e}\")\n        import traceback\n        traceback.print_exc()\n        return 1\n\n\nif __name__ == '__main__':\n    exit(main())\n","structuredPatch":[{"oldStart":163,"oldLines":7,"newStart":163,"newLines":7,"lines":["     # Research & Content Development\n- Gather all data in project `01-Research/` folder\n- Create detailed markdown outline in `02-Drafts/`\n- Include all content: comparison tables, cost analysis, recommendations\n- Format with clear structure (slide-by-slide breakdown)\n\n### 2. Configuration File Creation\n- Convert markdown outline to YAML configuration\n- Structure: title_slide + slides array\n- Slide types: `content`, `table`, `section_header`\n- Use color coding: 🟢 (advantage), 🟡 (adequate), 🔴 (concern)\n\n**Location:** Same folder as outline (`02-Drafts/`)\n\n**Example:**\n```yaml\ntitle_slide:\n  title: \"Presentation Title\"\n  subtitle: \"Presenter\\nDate\"\n\nslides:\n  - type: content\n    title: \"Slide Title\"\n    content:\n      - \"Bullet 1\"\n      - \"Bullet 2\"\n\n  - type: table\n    title: \"Comparison\"\n    columns: [\"Criteria\", \"Vendor A\", \"Vendor B\"]\n    rows:\n      - [\"Cost\", \"🟢 $100K\", \"🔴 $200K\"]\n```\n\n### 3. Automated Generation\n- Use script: `C:\\Users\\emarquez\\personal-claude-docs\\scripts\\generate_presentation.py`\n- Automatically cleans Safari template (keeps first/last slides)\n- Generates color-coded tables\n- Output to `02-Drafts/`\n\n**Command:**\n```powershell\ncd \"{project}\\02-Drafts\"\npy \"C:\\Users\\emarquez\\personal-claude-docs\\scripts\\generate_presentation.py\" `\n   config.yaml -o presentation.pptx\n```\n\n### 4. Create file in `youtube-analyses/` or update `best-practices/{domain}.md`\n2. Use standard templates with YAML metadata\n3. Tag with `implementation_status: documented`\n4. Rate `safari_relevance: high|medium|low`\n\n**Output:** Documented practice with metadata\n\n## Stage 3: PROMOTE\n\n**Input:** Documented practice with `safari_relevance: high`\n\n**Promotion Criteria:**\n- [ ] Practice is validated (tested in real work)\n- [ ] Practice has clear enforcement rules\n- [ ] Practice applies across multiple projects\n- [ ] Team agrees this should be standard\n\n**Actions:**\n1. Update `implementation_status: validated`\n2. Write enforcement rule in promotion format:\n   ```markdown\n   ## [Practice Name]\n\n   **Do:** [What to do]\n   **Don't:** [What not to do]\n   **Why:** [Reasoning]\n   **Source:** [Link to learning doc]\n   ```\n3. Add to `~/.claude/learning/promoted/` queue\n\n**Output:** Promotion-ready practice\n\n## Stage 4: ENFORCE\n\n**Input:** Promotion-ready practice\n\n**Target Locations:**\n\n| Scope | File | When to Use |\n|-------|------|-------------|\n| Global (all projects) | `~/.claude/CLAUDE.md` | Universal practices |\n| Safari projects | `safari-trace/.claude/CLAUDE.md` | Safari-specific |\n| Specific domain | Project CLAUDE.md | Project-specific |\n\n**Enforcement Levels:**\n\n| Level | Format in CLAUDE.md | Claude Behavior |\n|-------|---------------------|-----------------|\n| **MUST** | \"ALWAYS do X\" / \"NEVER do Y\" | Claude will follow strictly |\n| **SHOULD** | \"Prefer X over Y\" | Claude will default to this |\n| **MAY** | \"Consider X when...\" | Claude will use judgment |\n\n**Output:** Enforced practice in CLAUDE.md\n\n## Promotion Template\n\nWhen adding to CLAUDE.md, use this format:\n\n```markdown\n### [Practice Name]\n\n**Rule:** [MUST|SHOULD|MAY] [action]\n\n**Do:**\n- Specific action 1\n- Specific action 2\n\n**Don't:**\n- Anti-pattern 1\n- Anti-pattern 2\n\n**Why:** [Brief explanation]\n\n**Source:** [Link to learning/best-practices/{file}.md]\n```\n\n## Tracking Promotions\n\nUpdate `implementation-tracking/status.md` when promoting:\n\n```markdown\n| Practice | Source | Status | Promoted To | Date |\n|----------|--------|--------|-------------|------|\n| Component naming | ui-design.md | Enforced | global CLAUDE.md | 2026-01-18 |\n```\n\n## Quick Commands\n\n### Promote a Practice\n1. Verify practice in `best-practices/`\n2. Write enforcement rule\n3. Add to appropriate CLAUDE.md\n4. Prefix Safari-specific components with \"Safari\".\nStatus: validated\n```\n\n### After (in CLAUDE.md):\n```markdown\n### Component Naming Convention\n\n**Rule:** MUST use PascalCase for React components\n\n**Do:**\n- `SafariButton.tsx`\n- `UserProfileCard.tsx`\n- `DataTable.tsx`\n\n**Don't:**\n- `safari-button.tsx` (kebab-case)\n- `safarButton.tsx` (camelCase)\n- `Button.tsx` without Safari prefix for branded components\n\n**Why:** Consistency across codebase, easy identification of Safari-branded vs generic components\n\n**Source:** [best-practices/ui-design.md](~/.claude/learning/best-practices/ui-design.md)\n```\n\n---\n\n*This pipeline ensures learning doesn't stay as documentation - it becomes enforced behavior.*\n","numLines":167,"startLine":1,"totalLines":167}},"sourceToolAssistantUUID":"55579ec9-3f8b-4771-ae20-216ddbbd5d4b"}
